<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>Item 1.01 Entry Into A Material Definitive Agreement.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On December 11, 2022, Jiayi
Technologies (Xianning) Co., Ltd. (the &#8220;<b>Jiayi</b>&#8221;), a whole owned subsidiary of Planet Green Holdings Corp. (the &#8220;<b>Company</b>&#8221;),
entered into a Termination Agreement (the &#8220;<b>Termination Agreement</b>&#8221;) with Xiaodong Cai , Yongshen Chen (the &#8220;<b>Shareholders</b>&#8221;)
and Jilin Chuangyuan Chemical Co., Ltd. (the &#8220;<b>Jilin Chuangyuan</b>&#8221;), pursuant to which, among other things and subject
to the terms and conditions contained therein, Jiayi, the Shareholders and Jilin Chuangyuan agreed to terminate all of the rights and
obligations under the Amended and Restated Business Cooperation Agreement, the Consultation and Service Agreement, the Equity Option Agreement,
the Equity Pledge Agreement, and the Proxy Agreement (collectively, the &#8220;VIE Agreements&#8221;) entered among and between Jiayi,
the Shareholders and Jilin Chuangyuan on November 30, 2021. As a result of the completion of the transaction, the Company no longer consolidates
Jilin Chuangyuan&#8217;s financial statements into the financial statements of the Company for accounting purpose. The transaction was
completed on December 11, 2024. &#160;&#160; &#160;&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>Item 2.01 Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The information set forth
in Item 1.01 above relating to the closing of the VIE Agreements termination transaction is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>Item 9.01</b>&#160;<b>Financial Statements and Exhibits.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify">(d) Exhibits.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Party A, Party B, Party C and Party D hereby irrevocably agree and acknowledge that all of the Existing
Control Documents shall be terminated and have no effect as of the date of this Agreement.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&#30002;&#26041;&#12289;&#20057;&#26041;&#12289;&#19993;&#26041;&#21644;&#19969;&#26041;&#29305;&#27492;&#19981;&#21487;&#25764;&#38144;&#22320;&#21516;&#24847;&#24182;&#25215;&#35748;&#65292;&#25152;&#26377;&#29616;&#26377;&#25511;&#21046;&#25991;&#20214;&#33258;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#31614;&#35746;&#20043;&#26085;&#36215;&#32456;&#27490;&#19988;&#26080;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">As of the date of this Agreement, Party A, Party B, Party C and Party D shall no longer have any rights
under all and/or any of the Existing Control Documents, nor shall they be required to perform any obligations under all and/or any of
the Existing Control Documents.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#33258;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#31614;&#35746;&#20043;&#26085;&#36215;&#65292;&#30002;&#26041;&#12289;&#20057;&#26041;&#12289;&#19993;&#26041;&#21644;&#19969;&#26041;&#19981;&#20877;&#25317;&#26377;&#20840;&#37096;&#21644;</FONT>/<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#29616;&#26377;&#25511;&#21046;&#25991;&#20214;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#26435;&#21033;&#65292;&#20063;&#19981;&#20877;&#34987;&#35201;&#27714;&#23653;&#34892;&#25152;&#26377;&#21644;</FONT>/<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#29616;&#26377;&#25511;&#21046;&#25991;&#20214;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20041;&#21153;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Unless otherwise agreed in Article&nbsp;1.2 above, each of Party A, Party B, Party C and Party D hereby
irrevocably and unconditionally releases the Other Parties hereto from any disputes, claims, demands, rights, obligations, liabilities,
actions, contracts or causes of action of any kind or nature that it had, has or may have in the future, directly or indirectly, relating
to or arising out of all and/or any of the Existing Control Documents.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#38500;&#38750;&#19978;&#36848;&#31532;</FONT>1.2<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#26465;&#21478;&#26377;&#32422;&#23450;&#65292;&#30002;&#26041;&#12289;&#20057;&#26041;&#12289;&#19993;&#26041;&#21644;&#19969;&#26041;&#22343;&#19981;&#21487;&#25764;&#38144;&#22320;&#12289;&#26080;&#26465;&#20214;&#22320;&#20813;&#38500;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#22312;&#27492;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20105;&#35758;&#12289;&#32034;&#36180;&#12289;&#35201;&#27714;&#12289;&#26435;&#21033;&#12289;&#20041;&#21153;&#12289;&#36131;&#20219;&#12289;&#20854;&#26366;&#32463;&#12289;&#29616;&#22312;&#25110;&#23558;&#26469;&#21487;&#33021;&#30452;&#25509;&#25110;&#38388;&#25509;&#19982;&#25152;&#26377;&#21644;</FONT>/<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#29616;&#26377;&#25511;&#21046;&#25991;&#20214;&#30456;&#20851;&#25110;&#30001;&#20854;&#24341;&#36215;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#31181;&#31867;&#25110;&#24615;&#36136;&#30340;&#35785;&#35772;&#12289;&#21512;&#21516;&#25110;&#35785;&#35772;&#22240;&#30001;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Article
2</B> <B>Representations and Warranties</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 40pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -40pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>&#31532;</B></FONT><B>2<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#26465; &#38472;&#36848;&#19982;&#20445;&#35777;</FONT></B></P>

Parties as follow:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&#21508;&#26041;&#30340;&#38472;&#36848;&#21644;&#20445;&#35777;&#12290;&#19968;&#26041;&#29305;&#27492;&#21521;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#22768;&#26126;&#21644;&#20445;&#35777;&#22914;&#19979;&#65306;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">(1)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Such Party shall have the full right, power and authority to enter into this Agreement and all contracts
and documents to which it is a party as referred to herein, and the execution of this Agreement is of its true intent;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&#35813;&#26041;&#24212;&#25317;&#26377;&#31614;&#35746;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#21450;&#20854;&#20316;&#20026;&#19968;&#26041;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#25991;&#20214;&#30340;&#20805;&#20998;&#26435;&#21033;&#12289;&#26435;&#21147;&#21644;&#32844;&#26435;&#65292;&#24182;&#19988;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#30340;&#31614;&#32626;&#31526;&#21512;&#20854;&#30495;&#23454;&#24847;&#22270;&#65307;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Article 3</B> <B>Governing
Law and Dispute Resolution</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 40pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -40pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>&#31532;</B></FONT><B>3<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#26465; &#36866;&#29992;&#27861;&#24459;&#21644;&#20105;&#35758;&#35299;&#20915;</FONT></B></P>



<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">3.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The execution, effectiveness, interpretation, performance and dispute resolution shall be governed by
and interpreted in accordance with PRC laws.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#30340;&#25191;&#34892;&#12289;&#25928;&#21147;&#12289;&#35299;&#37322;&#12289;&#23653;&#34892;&#21644;&#20105;&#35758;&#35299;&#20915;&#22343;&#24212;&#36866;&#29992;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#24182;&#25353;&#20854;&#35299;&#37322;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">3.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Any and all disputes arising out of or in connection with the implementation of this Agreement shall be
resolved by the Parties through amicable negotiation.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&#22240;&#25191;&#34892;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#32780;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#25110;&#19982;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20105;&#35758;&#65292;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#36890;&#36807;&#21451;&#22909;&#21327;&#21830;&#35299;&#20915;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">3.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Any Party shall have the right to submit a dispute arising out of this Agreement to the China International
Economic and Trade Arbitration Commission (&ldquo;CIETAC&rdquo;) for arbitration in accordance with its arbitration rules&nbsp;and procedures
in effect at that time in Beijing. The arbitration tribunal shall consist of three arbitrators appointed in accordance with the arbitration
rules. The applicant and the respondent shall each appoint one arbitrator, and the third one shall be appointed by the two arbitrators
or by CIETAC. The arbitration shall be confidential and in Chinese. The arbitration award shall be final and binding on the Parties.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#22343;&#26377;&#26435;&#23558;&#22240;&#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#24341;&#36215;&#30340;&#20105;&#35758;&#25552;&#20132;&#20013;&#22269;&#22269;&#38469;&#32463;&#27982;&#36152;&#26131;&#20210;&#35009;&#22996;&#21592;&#20250;&#65288;</FONT>&ldquo;
CIETAC &rdquo;<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#65289;&#25353;&#29031;&#20854;&#24403;&#26102;&#22312;&#21271;&#20140;&#26377;&#25928;&#30340;&#20210;&#35009;&#35268;&#21017;&#21644;&#31243;&#24207;&#36827;&#34892;&#20210;&#35009;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#24237;&#30001;&#25353;&#29031;&#20210;&#35009;&#35268;&#21017;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#19977;&#21517;&#20210;&#35009;&#21592;&#32452;&#25104;&#12290;&#30003;&#35831;&#20154;&#21644;&#34987;&#30003;&#35831;&#20154;&#24212;&#21508;&#25351;&#23450;&#19968;&#21517;&#20210;&#35009;&#21592;&#65292;&#31532;&#19977;&#21517;&#20210;&#35009;&#21592;&#30001;&#20004;&#21517;&#20210;&#35009;&#21592;&#25110;&#30001;&#36152;&#20210;&#22996;&#25351;&#23450;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#24212;&#20445;&#23494;&#24182;&#20351;&#29992;&#20013;&#25991;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#35009;&#20915;&#20026;&#32456;&#23616;&#35009;&#20915;&#24182;&#23545;&#21508;&#26041;&#20855;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

the rights and obligations pending a final decision of any claim arising therefrom.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&#22312;&#20210;&#35009;&#26410;&#20915;&#26399;&#38388;&#65292;&#21508;&#26041;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#21033;&#21644;&#20041;&#21153;&#22343;&#24212;&#32487;&#32493;&#26377;&#25928;&#65292;&#20294;&#22240;&#20210;&#35009;&#32780;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#32034;&#36180;&#23578;&#26410;&#20316;&#20986;&#26368;&#32456;&#20915;&#23450;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#21644;&#20041;&#21153;&#38500;&#22806;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 40pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -40pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>&#31532;</B></FONT><B>4<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#26465;
